[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The crash in `aim_get_buddyname` is caused by two issues:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Unbounded `memcpy` using an attacker‐controlled `buddyname_length` against [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma fixed [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m-byte allocation.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Incorrect pointer arithmetic: copying from the start of the length field [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrather than the actual name bytes.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We will:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Read and validate the length field properly.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Bounds-check it against both the TVB’s remaining length and a reasonable [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaximum.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Allocate exactly [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m bytes for the name to accommodate a NUL [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mterminator.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Copy from the correct offset [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpast the length field[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • NUL-terminate the string.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This preserves existing dissection logic while eliminating the overflow.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Detailed patch plan [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `epan/dissectors/packet-aim.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Read the [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m-bit buddy-name length:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      guint16 buddyname_length = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_ntohs[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Advance the pointer past the length field:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      const gint name_offset = offset + [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mguint16[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m skip [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m bytes[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Validate `buddyname_length`:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Ensure the TVB actually contains that many bytes:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        guint tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_offset > tvb_len ||[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            buddyname_length > tvb_len - name_offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Malformed packet: length field exceeds available data *[0m[35m/[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          *name = NULL;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Optionally cap to a reasonable protocol maximum [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. [0m[1;36m512[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        const guint MAX_BUDDYNAME = [0m[1;36m512[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuddyname_length > MAX_BUDDYNAME[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          buddyname_length = MAX_BUDDYNAME;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Allocate and copy safely:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Allocate length+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m for NUL *[0m[35m/[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      *name = [0m[1;35mwmem_alloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpool, buddyname_length + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*name,[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mtvb_get_ptr[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, name_offset, buddyname_length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             buddyname_length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*name[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mbuddyname_length[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Return the validated/truncated `buddyname_length`.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preservation of existing logic[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We still return the buddy-name length, so callers such as [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_aim_chat_outgoing_msg` continue to compute offsets and parse messages [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In malformed cases, we return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m and `*name = NULL`, which causes downstream [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic to treat the name as empty but does not crash.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By validating against `tvb_reported_length`, we prevent reads beyond the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By capping or rejecting oversized lengths, we prevent blow-ups of the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated buffer.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adjusting the copy pointer to `offset + [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m` ensures the actual string data is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcopied, not the length bytes.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Null-terminating the result is a safety best practice and matches typical [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWireshark dissector patterns.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side effects and mitigation[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In the rare event of a truncated buddy name [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdue to capping[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, Wireshark will [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisplay a shortened name. This is preferable to a potential crash.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other dissectors or test harnesses are modified, ensuring existing tests [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand fuzz harnesses pass unchanged.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Upstream code that assumes names are NUL-terminated will continue to work [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar bounds-checking and `[0m[1;35mwmem_alloc[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, length + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` patterns appear in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mother dissecting routines in `packet-*.c`.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We avoid modifying any fuzz harness or external utilities per project policy.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn AddressSanitizer failure was triggered when fuzzing the AIM dissector in [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWireshark. The crash report shows a buffer overflow in the function [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`aim_get_buddyname` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-aim.[0m[1;92mc:591[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m due to an unchecked `memcpy` into a [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfixed-size buffer. A patch attempt replaced the fixed allocation with a [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength‐checked allocation and copy, introducing explicit bounds checks and a [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaximum buddy‐name length. After applying the patch, the build fails with a [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msigned/unsigned comparison error in packet-aim.c, and an unrelated warning appears [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39melsewhere. The build stops before producing a new binary.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzzing with libFuzzer and AddressSanitizer on the AIM protocol dissector [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`handler_aim`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m leads to an abort due to a fortified-`memcpy` failure.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The ASan log pinpoints the overflow to `aim_get_buddyname` in [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`packet-aim.[0m[1;92mc:591[0m[39m`, where a call to `[0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*name, [0m[1;35mtvb_get_ptr[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuddyname_length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` writes more bytes than the allocated buffer.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Stack trace:  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `__fortify_fail` → `__chk_fail` → `memcpy`  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `aim_get_buddyname` → `dissect_aim_chat_outgoing_msg` → `dissect_aim_snac` →[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m… → fuzz driver  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Removed the unbounded allocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mwmem_alloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpool, [0m[1;36m256[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and raw `memcpy`.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introduced:  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Reading `buddyname_length` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte field[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Compute `name_offset = offset + [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mguint16[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Retrieve `tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Bounds-check that `name_offset` and `buddyname_length` fit within `tvb_len` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Cap `buddyname_length` to a new `MAX_BUDDYNAME` of [0m[1;36m512[0m[39m bytes  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Allocate `buddyname_length + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` bytes via `wmem_alloc` and copy, then add a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNUL terminator  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Updated function signature remains the same [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreturns `buddyname_length` or [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mon error[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Result  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Build error in `packet-aim.c` at the new comparison:  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     “comparison of integers of different signs: ‘const gint’ and ‘guint’”  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Error emitted by `-Werror,-Wsign-compare`, stopping the compilation.  [0m         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`packet-hcrt.c` but does not halt the build.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
